<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">How to contribute</h2><a id="user-content-how-to-contribute" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How to contribute" href="#how-to-contribute"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">We welcome new contributors to the project whether you have changes to suggest, problems to report, or some feedback for us.
Please jump to the most relevant section from the list below:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Ask a question or offer feedback: use a <a href="#discussions">discussion</a></li>
<li>Suggest a change or report a problem: open an <a href="#issues">issue</a></li>
<li>Contribute a change to the repository: open a <a href="#pull-requests">pull request</a></li>
<li>Or just <a href="#get-in-touch">get in touch</a></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Discussions</h2><a id="user-content-discussions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Discussions" href="#discussions"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">We use <a href="https://github.com/OAI/OpenAPI-Specification/discussions?discussions_q=is%3Aopen">discussions</a> for anything that doesn't (yet) have a specific action associated with it.
Most ideas start as discussions.</p>
<p dir="auto">Please do come and start a discussion to:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>ask questions</li>
<li>make suggestions</li>
<li>give feedback</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Anyone can start a discussion and you're very welcome to do so! Write a message and pick a relevant discussion category.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Discussion management</h3><a id="user-content-discussion-management" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Discussion management" href="#discussion-management"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Participation in discussions and especially answering of questions is encouraged (and appreciated) by everyone.</p>
<p dir="auto">Discussions are closed when:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>the question has been answered.</li>
<li>no further action or conversation would be useful.</li>
<li>there has been no engagement for a while, or a previously popular thread has been inactive for an extended period.</li>
<li>activity is now taking place elsewhere, such as in an issue.</li>
<li>the discussion is out of scope for the project.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Issues</h2><a id="user-content-issues" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Issues" href="#issues"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Issues are for planned tasks, problems to solve, or requests for (specific) changes.
Most issues should have a clear outcome; something will be fixed, improved or otherwise measurably different when the issue is complete.</p>
<p dir="auto">We use <a href="#discussions">discussions</a> for ideas and early-stage suggestions.</p>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-note" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-info mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M0 8a8 8 0 1 1 16 0A8 8 0 0 1 0 8Zm8-6.5a6.5 6.5 0 1 0 0 13 6.5 6.5 0 0 0 0-13ZM6.5 7.75A.75.75 0 0 1 7.25 7h1a.75.75 0 0 1 .75.75v2.75h.25a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-2a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5h.25v-2h-.25a.75.75 0 0 1-.75-.75ZM8 6a1 1 0 1 1 0-2 1 1 0 0 1 0 2Z"></path></svg>Note</p><p dir="auto">For larger or more extensive changes, we have a formal <a href="#propose-a-specification-change">proposal process</a> to give more structure where it's needed.</p>
</div>
<p dir="auto">The best issues give a clear and concise explanation of the problem at hand, and ideally some examples of what the problem is.
Suggested solutions are also welcome, but it is very important that the issue outlines the problem that is being solved as well as the solution.
Some issues may be a backlog of a task that needs to be done; other issues might be automatically created as part of the project processes.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Issue management</h3><a id="user-content-issue-management" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Issue management" href="#issue-management"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">We have some issue automation to close inactive issues and create/pin/archive the weekly meeting issues.
More information is in the <a href="#appendix-issue-automation">Appendix: Issue automation</a> section.</p>
<p dir="auto">Everyone is encouraged to open and comment on issues in the project.
If you want to tag/assign/close something and you don't have enough permissions, add a comment and someone will help.</p>
<p dir="auto">Issues are managed by the <a href="#triage">Triage</a>, <a href="#maintainers">Maintainers</a> and <a href="#tsc">TSC</a> teams.
They may move issues to other repositories within the project as needed.</p>
<p dir="auto">In order to keep the issues list manageable and realistic for a relatively small group of volunteers, issues are proactively closed when it's not clear that they can be completed.
Issues may be closed when:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>they have been inactive for a long time</li>
<li>they are out of scope or no further constructive action can be taken</li>
<li>they are complete (yay!)</li>
<li>they are unclear and more details are not forthcoming</li>
<li>as a group, there is agreement that no further action will be taken</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">When issues are closed, a comment is added about why.
Closing issues is a reversible action, and it is always acceptable to comment and explain (politely) why an issue should not have been closed.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Labels</h3><a id="user-content-labels" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Labels" href="#labels"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">We make extensive use of labels.
The main categories are:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="https://github.com/OAI/OpenAPI-Specification/labels/Housekeeping">Housekeeping</a> for meetings, project logistics, etc.</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/OAI/OpenAPI-Specification/labels/approved%20pr%20port">approved pr port</a> for pull requests that repeat a change from one version to another</li>
<li>most other tags are used to group similar or related issues into topic areas; this list is ever-changing</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Labels related to <a href="#appendix-issue-automation">issue automation</a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="https://github.com/OAI/OpenAPI-Specification/labels/Needs%20attention">Needs attention</a> automated tag when an issue is updated</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/OAI/OpenAPI-Specification/labels/Needs%20author%20feedback">Needs author feedback</a> used to indicate that more information is needed from the issue creator</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/OAI/OpenAPI-Specification/labels/No%20recent%20activity">No recent activity</a> if no information is received, the issue is marked for closure (automatic after 30 days)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Milestones</h3><a id="user-content-milestones" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Milestones" href="#milestones"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">We use milestones in GitHub to plan what should be included in future releases.
Issues and pull requests should both be added to the earliest milestone we expect they will be released in.
Any changes that aren't ready in time for release should be moved to the next milestone or untagged.</p>
<p dir="auto">The milestones and items assigned to them are under constant review and subject to change.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Projects</h3><a id="user-content-projects" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Projects" href="#projects"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The OpenAPI Initiative uses GitHub Projects to manage work <em>outside</em> of the specification development process.  There are currently two active projects:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="https://github.com/orgs/OAI/projects/5/views/1">Contributor Guidance</a></li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/orgs/OAI/projects/4/views/1">Automation &amp; Infrastructure</a></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Pull requests</h2><a id="user-content-pull-requests" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Pull requests" href="#pull-requests"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-note" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-info mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M0 8a8 8 0 1 1 16 0A8 8 0 0 1 0 8Zm8-6.5a6.5 6.5 0 1 0 0 13 6.5 6.5 0 0 0 0-13ZM6.5 7.75A.75.75 0 0 1 7.25 7h1a.75.75 0 0 1 .75.75v2.75h.25a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-2a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5h.25v-2h-.25a.75.75 0 0 1-.75-.75ZM8 6a1 1 0 1 1 0-2 1 1 0 0 1 0 2Z"></path></svg>Note</p><p dir="auto">Since the 3.0.4 and 3.1.1 releases (October 2024), the OAS is developed in the <code>src/oas.md</code> file.
Check the <a href="#appendix-branch-strategy">Appendix: Branch Strategy</a> for more information about the updated branching strategy.</p>
</div>
<p dir="auto">Changes to the next version of the specification are welcome and can be proposed by anyone.</p>
<p dir="auto">For large changes that will need discussion, please use the <a href="#propose-a-specification-change">Proposal process</a>.
For other changes, we recommend <a href="#issues">opening an issue</a> first, so that you can get some feedback and any extra input you need before spending a lot of time on something.</p>
<p dir="auto">Schema changes are made on the same branch, but can be released independently.
When making a specification change for a new minor or major release that has a schema impact, including the schema change in the PR is preferred.
Patch releases cannot contain changes that <em>require</em> a schema update.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Use a fork</h3><a id="user-content-use-a-fork" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Use a fork" href="#use-a-fork"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">All work <strong>MUST be done on a fork</strong> and be submitted as a pull request.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Target the earliest active <code>*-dev</code> branch</h3><a id="user-content-target-the-earliest-active--dev-branch" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Target the earliest active *-dev branch" href="#target-the-earliest-active--dev-branch"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Branch from and submit pull requests to the a branch from the <em>earliest relevant and <a href="#active-branches">active</a></em> <code>vX.Y-dev</code> branch.
For example, if a change applies to both 3.1 and 3.2, the PR would go to the <code>v3.1-dev</code> branch, which will be merged up to <code>v3.2-dev</code> before the next 3.2 release.
All changes to the specification must conform to the <a href="/OAI/OpenAPI-Specification/blob/3.2.0/style-guide.md">style guide</a>.</p>
<p dir="auto">Both specification and schema changes follow this approach.</p>
<p dir="auto">For changes to repository files that affect all versions, use the <code>main</code> branch.
This might apply to, for example, Markdown files, automation, and scripts.</p>
<p dir="auto">For all pull requests, if they should not be merged yet for any reason (they depend on something else, you would like feedback from a specific reviewer), mark them as draft and they will not be merged while in that state.
Draft pull requests can still be reviewed while in draft state.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Preview specification HTML locally</h3><a id="user-content-preview-specification-html-locally" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Preview specification HTML locally" href="#preview-specification-html-locally"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-note" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-info mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M0 8a8 8 0 1 1 16 0A8 8 0 0 1 0 8Zm8-6.5a6.5 6.5 0 1 0 0 13 6.5 6.5 0 0 0 0-13ZM6.5 7.75A.75.75 0 0 1 7.25 7h1a.75.75 0 0 1 .75.75v2.75h.25a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-2a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5h.25v-2h-.25a.75.75 0 0 1-.75-.75ZM8 6a1 1 0 1 1 0-2 1 1 0 0 1 0 2Z"></path></svg>Note</p><p dir="auto"><code>npm run build-src</code> calls bash scripts. Use <a href="https://gitforwindows.org/" rel="nofollow">Git Bash</a> on Windows, or use the Windows Subsystem for Linux (WSL).</p>
</div>
<p dir="auto">The markdown source files are converted to HTML before publishing.
To do this locally, please</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Install <a href="https://nodejs.org/" rel="nofollow">Node.js</a></li>
<li>Check out this repo, go to the repo root, and switch to a development branch</li>
<li>Execute <code>npm install</code> (once, repeat after merging upstream changes)</li>
<li>Execute <code>npm run build-src</code> after changing <code>src/oas.md</code> (this first executes <code>npm run validate-markdown</code>, which can also be run separately)</li>
<li>Open output file <code>deploy-preview/oas.html</code> with a browser and check your changes</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">Please make sure the markdown validates and builds using the above steps before creating a pull request or marking a draft pull request as ready for review.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Reviewers</h2><a id="user-content-reviewers" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Reviewers" href="#reviewers"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-note" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-info mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M0 8a8 8 0 1 1 16 0A8 8 0 0 1 0 8Zm8-6.5a6.5 6.5 0 1 0 0 13 6.5 6.5 0 0 0 0-13ZM6.5 7.75A.75.75 0 0 1 7.25 7h1a.75.75 0 0 1 .75.75v2.75h.25a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-2a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5h.25v-2h-.25a.75.75 0 0 1-.75-.75ZM8 6a1 1 0 1 1 0-2 1 1 0 0 1 0 2Z"></path></svg>Note</p><p dir="auto">See also the detailed team outlines in the <a href="#roles">roles section</a>.</p>
</div>
<p dir="auto">All pull requests must be reviewed and approved by one member of the TSC or Maintainers teams.
Reviews from other contributors are always welcome.</p>
<p dir="auto">Additionally, all pull requests that change the specification file <code>src/oas.md</code> must be approved by two TSC members.</p>
<p dir="auto">Reviews requesting changes should have their changes addressed regardless of how many other approvers there are.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Publishing</h2><a id="user-content-publishing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Publishing" href="#publishing"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Specification Versions</h3><a id="user-content-specification-versions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Specification Versions" href="#specification-versions"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The specification versions are published to the <a href="https://spec.openapis.org" rel="nofollow">spec site</a> by creating an <code>vX.Y.Z-rel</code> branch where <code>src/oas.md</code> is renamed to the appropriate <code>versions/X.Y.Z.md</code> file and then merged to <code>main</code>.
This renaming on the <code>vX.Y.Z-rel</code> branch preserves the commit history for the published file on <code>main</code> when using <code>git log --follow</code> (as is the case for all older published files).</p>
<p dir="auto">The steps for creating a <code>vX.Y.Z-rel</code> branch are:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Update <code>EDITORS.md</code> on <code>main</code></li>
<li>Merge <code>main</code> into <code>dev</code> and <code>dev</code> into <code>vX.Y-dev</code> via PRs
<ul dir="auto">
<li>sync PRs are automatically created by workflows <code>sync-main-to-dev</code> and <code>sync-dev-to-vX.Y-dev</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Prepare spec files in <code>vX.Y-dev</code>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>npm run format-markdown</code></li>
<li><code>npm run build-src</code></li>
<li>open <code>deploy-preview/oas.html</code> in browser and verify correct formatting</li>
<li>adjust and repeat until done</li>
<li>merge changes to <code>src/oas.md</code> back into <code>vX.Y-dev</code> via PR</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Create <code>vX.Y.Z-rel</code> from <code>vX.Y-dev</code> and adjust it
<ul dir="auto">
<li>the bash script <code>scripts/adjust-release-branch.sh</code> does this:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>move file <code>src/oas.md</code> to <code>versions/X.Y.Z.md</code></li>
<li>copy file <code>EDITORS.md</code> to <code>versions/X.Y.Z-editors.md</code></li>
<li>delete folder <code>src/schemas</code></li>
<li>delete version-specific files and folders from <code>tests/schema</code>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>file <code>schema.test.mjs</code></li>
<li>folders <code>pass</code> and <code>fail</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Merge <code>vX.Y.Z-rel</code> into <code>main</code> via PR
<ul dir="auto">
<li>this PR should only add files <code>versions/X.Y.Z.md</code> and <code>versions/X.Y.Z-editors.md</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">The HTML renderings of the specification versions are generated from the <code>versions</code> directory on <code>main</code> by manually triggering the <a href="https://github.com/OAI/OpenAPI-Specification/blob/main/.github/workflows/respec.yaml"><code>respec</code> workflow</a>, which generates a pull request for publishing the HTML renderings to the <a href="https://spec.openapis.org" rel="nofollow">spec site</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Schema Iterations</h3><a id="user-content-schema-iterations" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Schema Iterations" href="#schema-iterations"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The schema iterations are published independently from the specification releases <a href="https://spec.openapis.org/#openapi-specification-schemas" rel="nofollow">in the schema section on the spec site</a>.
Schemas are updated in and directly published from the <code>vX.Y-dev</code> branches.</p>
<p dir="auto">As part of the publishing process, the YAML source files are converted to JSON, renamed to the relevant last-changed dates, and <code>WORK-IN-PROGRESS</code> placeholders are replaced with these dates as appropriate. This is usually done by the <code>schema-publish</code> workflow which detects changes on each <code>vX.Y-dev</code> branch, which generates a pull request for publishing the new schema iterations to the <a href="https://spec.openapis.org" rel="nofollow">spec site</a>. The workflow can also be run manually if required.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Release Process and Scope</h2><a id="user-content-release-process-and-scope" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Release Process and Scope" href="#release-process-and-scope"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This section relates to the 3.x versions only.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Minor Releases</h3><a id="user-content-minor-releases" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Minor Releases" href="#minor-releases"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Our roadmap for 3.x releases is community-driven, meaning the specification is open for proposed additions by anyone (see <a href="#propose-a-specification-change">Propose a Specification Change</a>), in addition to the issues already on the project backlog.</p>
<p dir="auto">Changes in minor releases (such as 3.2, 3.3) meet the following criteria:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Are <strong>backwards-compatible</strong> and be reasonably easy to implement in tooling that already supports the previous minor version.
For example, new optional fields can be added.</li>
<li>Drive quality-of-life improvements to support how OpenAPI is used by practitioners, so that OpenAPI evolves to continue to meet user needs.
For example, adding fields to support changes in other standards, or adopting common <code>x-*</code> extension fields into the specification.</li>
<li>Bring the future closer by making changes that are in line with future 3.x releases and the planned OpenAPI 4.x (Moonwalk) specification as the details of that become available.</li>
<li>Make the specification document clearer or easier to understand.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">A minor release is due when there are some meaningful features (including one or a small number of headline features).</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Patch Releases</h3><a id="user-content-patch-releases" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Patch Releases" href="#patch-releases"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Patch releases reflect a constant quest for improving the active minor versions of OpenAPI.
Since we do not edit specification documents after publication, even the smallest change has to be in a new release.</p>
<p dir="auto">Changes in patch releases meet the following criteria:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Editorial changes such as spelling or formatting fixes, including link updates.</li>
<li>Clarifications or additions that do not change the meaning of the specification.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Patch releases are created as often as there are changes to the specification worth releasing.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Release Process</h3><a id="user-content-release-process" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Release Process" href="#release-process"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A release requires a vote on the specification at a particular version and the associated release notes by TSC members within the voting period.
Major or minor release voting periods will be announced in the Slack channel and noted on the calendar at least 6 days in advance.
During this time, TSC members who have not yet voted must note their approval by leaving a comment on the GitHub pull request proposing the release; release notes should be included with the description.
TSC members are responsible for coordinating the information about the release to the outreach team as appropriate.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Patch-level releases require majority approval by TSC members. (Max voting period 3 days)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Minor: requires approval by 66% of TSC members. (Max voting period 7 days)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Major: requires approval by 66% of TSC members. (Max voting period 14 days)</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">During the voting period, further changes should not be made to the specification being considered.</p>
<p dir="auto">Once the threshold of approvals is met, the release can be performed by any TSC member.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Propose a Specification Change</h2><a id="user-content-propose-a-specification-change" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Propose a Specification Change" href="#propose-a-specification-change"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">As an organisation, we're open to changes, and these can be proposed by anyone.
The specification is very widely adopted, and there is an appropriately high bar for wide appeal and due scrutiny as a result.
We do not accept changes lightly (but we will consider any that we can).</p>
<p dir="auto">Small changes are welcome as pull requests.</p>
<p dir="auto">Bigger changes require a more formal process.</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Start a <a href="https://github.com/OAI/OpenAPI-Specification/discussions">discussion</a> of type "Enhancements".
The discussion entry must include some use cases, your proposed solution and the alternatives you have considered.
If there is engagement and support for the proposal over time, then it can be considered as a candidate to move to the next stage.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">It really helps to see the proposed change in action.
Start using it as a <code>x-*</code> extension if that's appropriate, or try to bring other evidence of your proposed solution being adopted.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">If you are adding support for something from another specification (such as OAuth), please point to implementations of that
specification so that we can understand how, and to what degree, it is being used.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">If the suggested change has good support, you will be asked to create a formal proposal.
Use the <a href="https://github.com/OAI/OpenAPI-Specification/tree/main/proposals">template in the proposals directory</a>, copy it to a new file, and complete it.
Once you the document is ready, open a pull request on the main branch.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">The proposal will be more closely reviewed and commented on or amended until it is either rejected or accepted.
At that point, the proposal is merged into the <code>main</code> branch and a pull request is opened to add the feature to the appropriate <code>dev</code> version of the specification.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">Questions are welcome on the process at any time. Use the discussions feature or find us in Slack.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Roles</h2><a id="user-content-roles" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Roles" href="#roles"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The OpenAPI project has some key roles that are played by multiple people.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">TSC</h3><a id="user-content-tsc" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: TSC" href="#tsc"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The Technical Steering Committee are listed in the <a href="/OAI/OpenAPI-Specification/blob/3.2.0/MAINTAINERS.md">MAINTAINERS file</a>.
They are the maintainers of the OpenAPI Specification itself and every other aspect of the project operation and direction.
TSC members can review changes to all parts of the repository and make decisions about the project.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Maintainers</h3><a id="user-content-maintainers" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Maintainers" href="#maintainers"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The maintainers have write access to the repository and play a key role in the project.
They review pull requests to non-specification parts of the repository, and take on other strategic tasks around project planning and maintenance.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Triage</h3><a id="user-content-triage" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Triage" href="#triage"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The triage team are active OpenAPI members who help with discussion and issue management.
They respond to new issues and discussions, direct people to our existing resources or raise conversations to a wider audience.
The triage team keeps an eye on the backlog and closes issues and discussions that are no longer active or needed.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Get in touch</h2><a id="user-content-get-in-touch" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Get in touch" href="#get-in-touch"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To get in touch with other people on the project, ask questions, or anything else:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Find us <a href="https://communityinviter.com/apps/open-api/openapi" rel="nofollow">on the OpenAPI Slack</a>.</li>
<li>Start a <a href="https://github.com/OAI/OpenAPI-Specification/discussions/">GitHub Discussion</a>.</li>
<li>Join one of our weekly meetings by checking the <a href="https://github.com/OAI/OpenAPI-Specification/issues?q=is%3Aissue%20state%3Aopen%20label%3AHousekeeping">issues list for an upcoming meetings</a>.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Appendix: Branch strategy</h2><a id="user-content-appendix-branch-strategy" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Appendix: Branch strategy" href="#appendix-branch-strategy"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For information on the branch and release strategy for OAS 3.0.4 and 3.1.1 and earlier, see the comments in <a href="https://github.com/OAI/OpenAPI-Specification/issues/3677" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/OAI/OpenAPI-Specification/issues/3677/hovercard">issue #3677</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Branch roles</h3><a id="user-content-branch-roles" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Branch roles" href="#branch-roles"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>main</code> is used to publish finished work and hold the authoritative versions of general documentation such as this document, which can be merged out to other branches as needed.  The <code>src</code> tree is <em><strong>not</strong></em> present on <code>main</code>.</li>
<li><code>dev</code> is the primary branch for working with the <code>src</code> tree.  Development infrastructure that is not needed on <code>main</code> is maintained here, and can be merged out to other non-<code>main</code> branches as needed.
Changes on <code>main</code> are automatically included in a pull request to <code>dev</code> (see the (section on <a href="#branch-sync-automation">branch sync</a>).</li>
<li><code>vX.Y-dev</code> is the minor release line development branch for X.Y, including both the initial X.Y.0 minor version and all subsequent X.Y.Z patch versions.  All PRs are made to oldest active <code>vX.Y-dev</code> branch to which the change is relevant, and then merged forward as shown in the diagram further down in this document.</li>
<li><code>vX.Y.Z-rel</code> is the release branch for an X.Y.Z release (including when Z == 0).  It exists primarily for <code>git mv</code>-ing <code>src/oas.md</code> to the appropriate <code>versions/X.Y.Z.md</code> location and removing schema-related files before merging back to <code>main</code>, and can also be used for any emergency post-release fixes that come up, such as when a 3rd party changes URLs in a way that breaks published links.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Branching and merging (3.1.2, 3.2.0, and later)</h3><a id="user-content-branching-and-merging-312-320-and-later" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Branching and merging (3.1.2, 3.2.0, and later)" href="#branching-and-merging-312-320-and-later"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Upon release:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Pre-release steps:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The most recent <em>published</em> patch release from the previous line is merged up to <code>vX.Y-dev</code>, if relevant</li>
<li>If doing simultaneous releases on multiple lines, do them from the oldest to newest line</li>
<li>For example, if releasing 3.1.3 and 3.2.0:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>release 3.1.3 first</li>
<li>release 3.2.0 second</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Release branching and merging:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>branch <code>vX.Y.Z-rel</code> from <code>vX.Y-dev</code> (same commit that was merged to <code>dev</code> if relevant)</li>
<li>After renaming <code>src/oas.md</code> to <code>versions/X.Y.Z.md</code> and <a href="#specification-versions">other adjustments</a>, merge <code>vX.Y.Z-rel</code> to <code>main</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Publishing to the <a href="https://spec.openapis.org" rel="nofollow">spec site</a> is triggered by the merge to <code>main</code></li>
<li>Post-release steps:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>If this was a major or minor release (Z == 0), branch <code>vX.Y+1-dev</code> from <code>vX.Y-dev</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><em>Release lines are grouped by color, although the colors of <code>dev</code> and <code>main</code> are not significant as these diagrams are limited to only 8 colors.</em></p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Branch sync automation</h3><a id="user-content-branch-sync-automation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Branch sync automation" href="#branch-sync-automation"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To keep changes in sync, we have some GitHub actions that open pull requests to take changes from <code>main</code> onto the <code>dev</code> branch, and from <code>dev</code> to each active version branch.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>sync-main-to-dev</code> opens a pull request with all the changes from the <code>main</code> branch that aren't yet included on <code>dev</code>.</li>
<li><code>sync-dev-to-vX.Y-dev</code> opens pull requests with all the changes from <code>dev</code> that aren't yet included on the corresponding <code>vX.Y-dev</code> branch.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">These need a single approval from either maintainers or TSC and can be merged.
The aim is to bring build script and repository documentation changes to the other branches.
Published versions of the specifications and schemas will also move across branches with this approach.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Appendix: Issue Automation</h2><a id="user-content-appendix-issue-automation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Appendix: Issue Automation" href="#appendix-issue-automation"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Automated closure of issues Process</h3><a id="user-content-automated-closure-of-issues-process" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Automated closure of issues Process" href="#automated-closure-of-issues-process"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In an effort to keep the list of issues up to date and easier to navigate through, issues get closed automatically when they become inactive.</p>
<p dir="auto">This process makes use of the following labels:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>Needs author feedback</code>: the issue has been replied to by the triage team and is awaiting a follow up from the issue's author. This label needs to be added manually by people doing triage/experts whenever they reply. It's removed automatically by the workflow.</li>
<li><code>No recent activity</code>: the issue hasn't received a reply from its author within the last 10 days since <code>Needs author feedback</code> was added and will be closed within 28 days if the author doesn't follow up. This label is added/removed automatically by the workflow.</li>
<li><code>Needs attention</code>: The issue's author has replied since the <code>Needs author feedback</code> label was set and the triage team will reply as soon as possible. This label needs to be removed manually by people doing triage/experts whenever they reply. It's added automatically by the workflow.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Automated TDC agenda issues Process</h3><a id="user-content-automated-tdc-agenda-issues-process" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Automated TDC agenda issues Process" href="#automated-tdc-agenda-issues-process"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">An issue is opened every week, 7 days in advance, for the Technical Developer Community (TDC), it provides the information to connect the meeting, and serves as a placeholder to build the agenda for the meeting. Anyone is welcome to attend the meeting, or to add items to the agenda as long as they plan on attending to present the item. These issues are also automatically pinned for visibility and labeled with "Housekeeping".</p>
<p dir="auto">Ten (10) days after the meeting date is passed (date in the title of the issue), it gets closed and unpinned automatically.</p>
</article></div><div class="d-none"></div></section></div></div></div> </div> <!-- --> </div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="ScrollMarksContainer-module__scrollMarksContainer__Eu7uU" id="find-result-marks-container"></div><div class="d-none"></div><div class="d-none"></div></div> <!-- --> <!-- --> </div>
</react-app>


  </div>

</turbo-frame>

    </main>
  </div>

  </div>
